visualization of inflected forms and vocab that students should know after 7 chapters of First Greek Book modified for Thucydides

This visualization represents all 150,000 words from Thucydides.

Green words: students have seen the vocab word and the morphology. Students should be able to parse and translate a Greek form. Given an English definition and a form, students should be able to generate the correct form.

Blue words: students have seen the morphology but not the vocab word. Students should be able to parse any of these forms and to create an appropriate translation given a gloss (e.g., from "throw" to "they throw", given a third plural form).

Red words: students have seen the vocab word but not the morphlogy. If we add the dictionary word as a gloss, students should be able to recognize the meaning of the word. This exercise probably only makes sense if we present an aligned English translation where we replace the English equivalent with the dictionary word that the students know.

Where students have not encountered either the vocabulary word or the morphology, the words are represented as a period.

The visualization is quite simplistic. The eight books of Thucydides are represented as 8 cells in a table. If your browser breaks the lines, then you may see book 2. If your browser places every book/chapter on a single line, then you wil have to scroll to the right to see the other books. If you are looking at this on smart phone....

This visualization does not deal with ambiguity and assumes that a form can be from any of its morphological analyses.
